        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer636499152" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11212969102666835714">Even more vicious, clever, and disturbing than the first novel. This book takes a lighter tone overall (though all the TRIGGER WARNINGS from the first one-- rape, child abuse, torture-- still apply). I have read this book over more times than I can count, and I still laugh, gasp, and fist-pump at the same spots as always. My favorite character from the first one barely made an appearance, sadly, but I have a new favorite now, and I won't name her; I'll just say "kiss, kiss" and smile wickedly...</span>
  <span id="freeText11212969102666835714" style="display:none">Even more vicious, clever, and disturbing than the first novel. This book takes a lighter tone overall (though all the TRIGGER WARNINGS from the first one-- rape, child abuse, torture-- still apply). I have read this book over more times than I can count, and I still laugh, gasp, and fist-pump at the same spots as always. My favorite character from the first one barely made an appearance, sadly, but I have a new favorite now, and I won't name her; I'll just say "kiss, kiss" and smile wickedly...<br /><br />I should mention that, as much as I adore this series, and the first two books in particular, I have to agree with every single criticism I've seen of them. Yes, the characters are archetypes more than individuals. Yes, there is more DRAMA than you can find on prime-time TV shows meant for teens. Yes, Bishop repeats herself, a lot. She can be more heavy-handed than a champion boxer. Non-heterosexual love isn't a possibility in her universe. Everything is made larger than life to the point where it's absurd if you look too closely-- and maybe even if you don't. The details of how magic works in her world aren't even remotely self-consistent.<br /><br />You either love these books or you hate them. I happen to love them.<br /><br />These aren't fantasy novels-- they are mythology epics with candy lips and vampire teeth. They are erotic dreams that only feel real while you are inside them. They are overripe hallucinogenic fruits on the verge of being rotten, sharp and sweet and rich and dense. I understand why some people spit them out. But I personally just can't get enough.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11212969102666835714" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/395599-shannon-giraffe-days?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/395599-shannon-giraffe-days?shelf=favourite">favourite</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer13936058" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1947485119736621347">Jaenelle, the living embodiment of magic, the prophesied Witch, is a young girl of twelve tormented by the horrors she endured at the hands of her relatives - from which Daemon Sadi rescued her. Her physical wounds are healing, but mentally she may never recover.<br/><br/>As she rests in the home of the High Lord of Hell, she learns trust and love and befriends other creatures - who come to her for help as their realm is invaded, their land taken from them. She will never be alone though, with Daemon and </span>
  <span id="freeText1947485119736621347" style="display:none">Jaenelle, the living embodiment of magic, the prophesied Witch, is a young girl of twelve tormented by the horrors she endured at the hands of her relatives - from which Daemon Sadi rescued her. Her physical wounds are healing, but mentally she may never recover.<br /><br />As she rests in the home of the High Lord of Hell, she learns trust and love and befriends other creatures - who come to her for help as their realm is invaded, their land taken from them. She will never be alone though, with Daemon and his half-brother Lucivar beside her, and Saetan as her surrogate father, protecting her from those who wish to abuse and manipulate her.<br /><br />The wondrous things about Bishop's debut trilogy is the depth of its character development, the richness and originality of its world, and the maturity and unpredictability of its plot. You can't help but grow attached to the characters, and feel what they feel.<br /><br />At the same time, it's exciting - never dull - and will take you to places few fantasy books touch upon. Nothing is black-and-white, everything will make you question your assumptions, and Jaenelle has to be the most endearing, unprepossessing heroine you're likely to read in fantasy. Masterfully written.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1947485119736621347" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Megan Krogh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Megan Krogh" href="/user/show/28086102-megan-krogh">Megan Krogh</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1922795174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7351162716298647477"><i>Continued from the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1608666507?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Daughter of the Blood</a> review page (because my review was too long; I explain my predicament on the Daughter of the Blood review page)</i><br/><br/><i>Titian:</i><br/>HOLY FUCK I LOVE TITIAN!!!!!!! (let me say it louder for the people in the back) <i>
  <u>
    <b>HOLY FUCK I LOVE TITIAN!!!!!!!!!!!!!</b>
  </u>
</i><br/>SHE IS SUCH A BEAUTIFUL, FIERCE, INDEPENDENT FEMINIST AND I JUST LOVE IT SO FUCKING MUCH!!!!!!!! IM JUST CRYING RIGHT NOW CAUSE SHE’S SO BEAUTIFUL! LIKE, SHE IS THE PERSON WHO I ASPIRE TO BE--ULTIMATE ROLE MODEL </span>
  <span id="freeText7351162716298647477" style="display:none"><i>Continued from the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1608666507?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Daughter of the Blood</a> review page (because my review was too long; I explain my predicament on the Daughter of the Blood review page)</i><br><br><i>Titian:</i><br>HOLY FUCK I LOVE TITIAN!!!!!!! (let me say it louder for the people in the back) <i>
  <u>
    <b>HOLY FUCK I LOVE TITIAN!!!!!!!!!!!!!</b>
  </u>
</i><br>SHE IS SUCH A BEAUTIFUL, FIERCE, INDEPENDENT FEMINIST AND I JUST LOVE IT SO FUCKING MUCH!!!!!!!! IM JUST CRYING RIGHT NOW CAUSE SHE’S SO BEAUTIFUL! LIKE, SHE IS THE PERSON WHO I ASPIRE TO BE--ULTIMATE ROLE MODEL RIGHT HERE LADIES AND GENTLEMEN!!! AND THE WAY SHE DOESN’T PUT UP WITH SAETAN’S BULLSHIT, I MEAN SHIT, SHE WAS GOING TO KILL <i>THE HIGH LORD OF HELL</i> BECAUSE SHE THOUGHT THAT SAETAN DIDN’T PROTECT JAENELLE AND JAENELLE WAS DEAD! ALSO (drumroll please) LET’S TALK ABOUT HOW TITIAN <i>FUCKING SLAUGHTERS</i> GREER!!!!!!!!!!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528958.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I MEAN SHIT SHE FIRST<br>1) DRIVES AN ARROW INTO HIS BODY AND PINS HIM TO A TREE<br>2) STARTS CARVING THE SKIN FROM HIS BONES<br>3) TEARS HIS LIMBS FROM HIS TORSO<br>4) DIGS HIS GUTS OUT OF HIS TORSO<br>5) OPENS HIS HEAD <br>6) LETS THE HOUNDS FEAST ON HIS BRAIN <u>
  <b>(HIS FUCKING BRAIN!!!!)</b>
</u><br>7) WALKS AWAY LIKE A FUCKING BADASS!!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1483248775ra/21593404.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452106693ra/17648362.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>LIKE IF THERE WAS A WAY FOR GREER TO GO, THAT IS THE MOST PERFECT ONE!!!!! I MEAN, NOT ONLY DID HE RAPE JAENELLE, BUT PROBABLY MORE WOMEN TOO. PLUS, HE ALSO KILLED TITIAN, SO <u>
  <b>BITCH FUCKING SLAAAAYYYYY!!!!!!!!!!!!</b>
</u><br><br><i>The Coven/The First Circle:</i><br>Also known as: Squad goals™, Dream team™, also (if you’ve read A Court of Mist and Fury), the Court of Dreams #2. I am just fully in love with this beautiful, wholesome court. Jaenelle deserves this so much and *wipes away tear* i-it’s just so-o a-amazi-innnngg!!!!!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468905646ra/19756677.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Not only does Jaenelle literally rule like 99% of Kaeleer cause they all yielded to her, but she even has the Kindred and it’s just so--<i>wholesome</i>. Like when you even have fucking <i>animals</i> on your side, you know this ho gonna be one Badass Motherfucker™ who you <i>do not</i> want to mess with. <br>But I loved when they all came that summer (the <i>whole</i> summer. I know, Saetan wanted to kill himself, it was hilarious!). And when that one artist, Dujae wanted Saetan to give his soul to the Darkness cause he didn’t want to live anymore, and Karla and Jaenelle barge in and pretty much tell Dujae that he isn’t going to do that cause they need an artist. And he’s just like “....uh, okay.” <br><blockquote>“Is your ego so puffed up that it’s beneath you to teach a few little witches how to draw?” Karla asked with sweet malevolence.<br>“Puffed up? No, no, Ladies, I would be honored but--”<br>“But?” Jaenelle asked softly in her midnight voice.<br>Dujae shuddered. Saetan shivered.<br>“I am a demon.”<br>Silence.<br>Finally Karla snorted, “If you don’t want to teach us, just say so, but stop using a paltry excuse to weasel out of it.”</blockquote><br>And when they leave the room, Dujae pretty much tells Saetan:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528959.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But because of them, he finds his purpose again and doesn’t want to go into the Darkness. <br><br>But anyways, the First Circle is literally Goals. Go keeps on supported Jaenelle you guys!<br><br><u>
  <b>Plot:</b>
</u><br>Okay, so we finally made it to the plot (wow! That took awhile! I mean, if you think this is long just reading it, how do you think I feel? I actually had to think of and type all of this!). So a lot of this I used in my Characters, so there will be a few holes. <br><br>So let’s start with MY TWO BEAUTIFUL SONS FIGHTING AND HATING EACH OTHER CAUSE OF FALSE INFORMATION LIKE DAEMON CAME TO GET LUCIVAR OUT OF THE SALT MINES BUT LUCIVAR THOUGHT DAEMON WAS THE ONE WHO HAD RAPED JAENELLE AND HE HATED HIM (and thus has to stay in the mines for 5 more years) AND IT WAS JUST SO SAD LIKE WHY YOU GOTTA DO THIS TO ME BISHOP!?!?!!?<br><br>And then FUCKING HEKATAH MAKING MY BEAUTIFUL, SWEET DAEMON FALL INTO THE TWISTED KINGDOM LIKE WHAT THE FUCKING YOU PIECE OF SHIT?! HOW DARE YOU!!! MY SON WAS DOING NOTHING BUT TRYING TO FIND JAENELLE AND JUST HAD TO ONCE AGAIN FUCK <i>EVERYTHING</i> UP, LIKE GOD DAMN GIRL GET A FUCKING HOBBY!!<br><br>Then Lucivar finally escapes from the mines (cause he wants to die and his wings are nothing now and he still hates Daemon and he thinks his Queen is dead and whhhyyyyy). And that Zuultah bitch tried to stop him but he was just like:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528960.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And he tries to make that suicide run and kill himself<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492560259i/22528961._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>MY DARLING JAENELLE IS STILL ALIVE DON’T DO THIS TO YOURSELF!!! <br>But then THEY FINALLY REUNITE!!!!! (okay for once these caps were happy caps) AND IT’S SO AMAZING AND BEAUTIFUL!!!!<br><br>Okay, but backing up a little bit. I was so fucking pissed when that stupid fucking Dark Council tried to take Jaenelle away from Saetan. LIKE HOS, THIS MAN IS THE BEST THING THAT HAS HAPPENED IN HER LIFE, DO NOT TRY TO TAKE HER AWAY FROM HIM! But then Jaenelle ain’t havin’ that shit and SHE FUCKING STOPS THE SUN FROM RISING LIKE GADAMN GIRL WAY TO BE SO EXTRA I FUCKING LOVE IT<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528962.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>AND THEN HEKATAH AND HER FUCKING BULLSHIT HAPPENS AGAIN AND SHE TRIES TO MARRY JAENELLE OFF BUT THEN JAENELLE FLIPS HER SHIT AND FUCKING INCINERATES THE GUY TRYING TO MARRY HER!!<br><br>And then Lucivar and Jaenelle are in the woods, trying to clear the safframate from her system and it’s excruciatingly painful for her (all cause of The Bitch™)<br><br>AND BAM, HEKATAH TRIES TO FUCK SHIT UP <i>AGAIN</i> (BITCH 👏GET👏A👏FUCKING👏HOBBY<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528963.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> )<br>AND KILL LUCIVAR (not knowing Jaenelle is with him) BY SENDING THOUSANDS OF JHINKA TO KILL HIM<br>BUT JAENELLE IS THERE AND 1) SHE’S TRYING TO RECOVER FROM THE SAFFRAMATE 2) HEALS OVER <i>300</i> LANDEN AND THEN WHEN LUCIVAR KNOWS THEY ARE GOING TO DIE CAUSE THERE ARE 6,000 JHINKA AND JAENELLE COMES OUT AND JUST FUCKING SLAUGHTERS THEM IN <i>30 FUCKING SECONDS!!!!!!! SIX-FUCKING-THOUSAND</i> IN <i>THIRTY-FUCKING-SECONDS!!!!!!!!!!!!!!</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528964.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Holy FUCK is Janelle powerful!<br><br>And thus, Hekatah’s plan at getting Lucivar killed and out of the way fails… oh no!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528965.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>YEAH BITCH, SUCK IT!!<br><br>AND THEN SHE LOSES HER BEAUTY AND LOOKS LIKE A FUCKING ROTTED CORPSE!!!!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528966.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>AND THEN MY SON FINALLY STARTED TO CLIMB OUT OF THE TWISTED KINGDOM<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528967.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>AND MY HEART MELTED AND I WAS SO HAPPY I JUMPED UP AND DID A LITTLE DANCE!!!!!!<br><br>And then I cried. <br><br>Hundreds of unicorns were slaughtered. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528968.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I felt as if the sun stopped shining as brightly. Like the world slowed down a little. My heart broke and I literally started sobbing (thank God I was at home or that would have been reeeaaally embarrassing!)<br><br>And then I read what had happened to Kaetien. He was the first unicorn that Saetan and his household had ever seen. I still remember the joy Saetan and Andulvar had felt and shared at seeing Kaetien on their lawn that morning. Out of all the Blood in the book to kill, why did Bishop have to kill the unicorns?<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492560259i/22528969._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I had to put the book down when I read that scene. This was the only scene (of sad tears) that made me put this book in my “Cried” bookshelf.<br>But this was the final straw for Jaenelle. This was the moment that Jaenelle knew she had to set up her court (and become the baddest bitch)<br><br>Well, I mean, first Jaenelle goes to the Dark Council and tells them to stop, but fucking Jorval says that since she doesn’t rule any Territories, she doesn’t have a justifiable complaint.<br>So Jaenelle’s just like:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528970.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>“I’m going to make the Offering to the Darkness and set up my court.”</blockquote><br>But when all of Jaenelle’s friends and family gather in the throne room and DRACA TURNS OUT TO BE THE QUEEN FROM THE BEGINNING OF TIME LIKE WOW WHAT A FUCKING TWIST I DID NOT SEE THAT COMING AT ALL, I MEAN WHEN SAETAN TOLD THE STORY TO TITIAN AND HE EVEN MENTIONS THAT THE BOOKS NEVER TOLD THE QUEEN’S NAME, I THOUGHT IT WAS KIND OF FISHY, BUT FOR DRACA TO BE THE QUEEN FROM THE BEGINNING OF TIME?!!?!?!!?!?! WOW!!!!!!!!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470539900ra/19939111.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>AND JAENELLE FORMS HER BADASS COURT AND <b>
  <i>WEARS A FUCKING EBONY JEWEL LIKE OH MY GOOOOOODDDDD!!!!!!!!!!!</i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528971.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>THEN RIGHT AFTER JAENELLE MARCHES RIGHT TO THE STUPID DARK COUNCIL AND GOES THE FUCK <b>
  <i>OFF!!!!!!!!!!</i>
</b> <br><blockquote>“That is a list of the Territories that yielded ot Ebon Askavi. They now stand in the shadow of the Keep. They are mine. Anyone who tries to settle in my Territory without my consent will be dealt with. Anyone who harms any of my people will be executed. There will be no excuses and no exceptions. I will say it simply so that the members of this Council and the intruders who thought to take the land they had no right to claim can never say they misunderstood.” Jaenelle’s lips curled into a snarl. “STAY OUT OF MY TERRITORY!”</blockquote><br>DAMN BITCH FUCKING SLAAAAYYYY YAAAAAAAASSSSSSS!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br>But before hand when she first walks into the meeting and some stupid bitch has the <i>audacity</i> to whine: “Why is <i>she</i> allowed to have a unicorn’s horn? <i>I</i> wasn’t allowed to have one as compensation for my men being killed.”<br>And that horn was Kaetien’s. I was literally ready to fight that dumb bitch. LET’S GO! SQUARE THE FUCK UP!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528972.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But for once in this series (which, I mean, isn’t saying a lot since this is only the second book), there is actually a happy ending. Jaenelle has her court and friends and family who love her. Saetan is Steward of Jaenelle’s court and has a daughter. Lucivar has a Queen he can respect and is First Escort and Warlord Prince of Ebon Rih. DAEMON IS CLIMBING OUT OF THE TWISTED KINGDOM AND COMING BACK HOME. Surreal is...doin’ her thing and...not dying. Hekatah is a rotting corpse who has to go into hiding. Greer is dead. Jorval is...well, still shit, but he got knocked down a few pegs. TITIAN IS STILL AN AMAZING BADASS. Jaenelle’s court is Squad goals™. And Jaenelle pretty much rules most of Kaeleer (like, yeah Bitch Jorval, who rules all these Territories now? Who has a justifiable complaint now? Huh, huh? Bitch.).<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492560259ra/22528973.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, congrats, you finally made it to the end of my review! This is probably my longest review so far, and I probably won’t be doing it again, so rest easy. But I’m glad you read it and I hope you loved this book as much as I did! I’m sorry I had to start it on the Daughter of the Blood review page and it got all confusing (believe me I was pissed when I found that I had written too long of a review) But anyways, recommend this series to everyone you know because I don’t think it gets enough credit.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492560259i/22528974.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482412891ra/21514658.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="7351162716298647477" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2464045470" />
    <a title="Autumn Miller ~ autumnbookreads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66604997-autumn-miller-autumnbookreads"><img alt="Autumn Miller ~ autumnbookreads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528222708p2/66604997.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2464045470?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Autumn Miller ~ autumnbookreads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Autumn Miller ~ autumnbookreads" href="/user/show/66604997-autumn-miller-autumnbookreads">Autumn Miller ~ autumnbookreads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66604997-autumn-miller-autumnbookreads?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2464045470" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15899736405327658293"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/26897.Anne_Bishop' title='Anne Bishop' rel='nofollow noopener'>Anne Bishop</a> has done it again. She has made me fall in love with yet another one of her books. This was a perfect sequel to the first book, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9953540.Daughter_of_The_Blood__The_Black_Jewels___1_' title='Daughter of The Blood (The Black Jewels, #1) by Anne Bishop' rel='nofollow noopener'>Daughter of The Blood</a>. Anything that was lacking in the first book (which wasn't much) was put into this second installment. This definitely exceeded my expectations (which were pretty high to begin with). Obviously, I will be reading the next book, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/47959.Queen_of_the_Darkness__The_Black_Jewels___3_' title='Queen of the Darkness (The Black Jewels, #3) by Anne Bishop' rel='nofollow noopener'>Queen of the Darkness</a>.<br/>SIDE NOTE: I find it extremely interesting that, while Jaenelle is the main character, w</span>
  <span id="freeText15899736405327658293" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/26897.Anne_Bishop" title="Anne Bishop" rel="nofollow noopener">Anne Bishop</a> has done it again. She has made me fall in love with yet another one of her books. This was a perfect sequel to the first book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9953540.Daughter_of_The_Blood__The_Black_Jewels___1_" title="Daughter of The Blood (The Black Jewels, #1) by Anne Bishop" rel="nofollow noopener">Daughter of The Blood</a>. Anything that was lacking in the first book (which wasn't much) was put into this second installment. This definitely exceeded my expectations (which were pretty high to begin with). Obviously, I will be reading the next book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/47959.Queen_of_the_Darkness__The_Black_Jewels___3_" title="Queen of the Darkness (The Black Jewels, #3) by Anne Bishop" rel="nofollow noopener">Queen of the Darkness</a>.<br />SIDE NOTE: I find it extremely interesting that, while Jaenelle is the main character, we haven't gotten her point of view. Everyone around her (including the villains) have gotten one and I am really curious why <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/26897.Anne_Bishop" title="Anne Bishop" rel="nofollow noopener">Anne Bishop</a> decided to write this that way.</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_35645115" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/35645115" />
    <a title="Katie(babs)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs"><img alt="Katie(babs)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1242522005p2/179852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/35645115?book_show_action=true">Oct 18, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie(babs)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie(babs)" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs">Katie(babs)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer35645115" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18367620797633809101">The second book, Heir to the Shadows, is a very, very different book from the first in the series. Daughter of Blood was so graphic in its telling. It was truly an uncomfortable read. But Heir to the Shadows is a bit more calm and hopeful. Hopeful in the sense that even thought certain characters are still separated from one another (Daemon and Jaenelle) and their enemies are still free and planning to destroy them, Anne gives her readers hope that when all is said and done, there will be peace </span>
  <span id="freeText18367620797633809101" style="display:none">The second book, Heir to the Shadows, is a very, very different book from the first in the series. Daughter of Blood was so graphic in its telling. It was truly an uncomfortable read. But Heir to the Shadows is a bit more calm and hopeful. Hopeful in the sense that even thought certain characters are still separated from one another (Daemon and Jaenelle) and their enemies are still free and planning to destroy them, Anne gives her readers hope that when all is said and done, there will be peace and happiness across the land, much like the fairy tales we have read when we are children. The prince will find the princess, even though he must battle evil and fight for the right for her love. Of course the prince and princess I am thinking in these terms are Daemon and Janelle. Where as in Daughter of the Blood, they went through more physical traumas, in Heir to the Shadows, these two are so lost and feel unworthy. They refuse the acceptance within themselves and the others around them. Even though Jaenelle and Daemon now have a wonderful support system that includes family and friends, they seem to turn away from the love given to them. And even though the fates say these two belong together, there are many outside forces keeping them apart.<br /><br />Heir to the Shadows begins two years after Daughter of the Blood has ended. Jaenelle is still in her coma like state. Her body has healed but her mind is lost in the Abyss. Saeten appeals to the Dark Council and is granted for the right to be her guardian, essentially her foster father. Saeten is able to enter into the Abyss and find Jaenelle and bring her out. Unfortunately Jaenelle has some memory loss and does not remember everything that has happened to her. She does not remember Daemon or how he went into the Abyss to save her. Both Jaenelle and Witch (the side of her that will bring peace and is dreams made flesh) have pushed her rape and molestation, deep down inside of her. And because of that, Daemon is suffering horribly.<br /><br />Daemon is in the Twisted Kingdom, where his mind is lost, much like Jaenelle’s. But whereas Jaenelle’s was on a vacation of sorts, Daemon has gone insane from the grief over his one true love. He has distorted the events of when he went to save Witch Because his brother Lucivar accuses Daemon of taking advantage of Jaenelle/Witch, by seducing the then twelve year old in the Abyss, Daemon’s grief holds no bounds. Jaenelle has been brought back to the living, much like Lazarus rising from his grave. Daemon is buried, perhaps forever, unless Jaenelle can save him.<br /><br />You are probably wondering why Saeten does not try to find his son and save him like he did Jaenelle. Saeten doesn’t know what has happened to Daemon, and in part, he is afraid that if he tells Jaenelle, she made have a relapse. So instead, Saeten lets Jaenelle heal until she is strong both in mind and in spirit to tell her about her mate. During this time Jaenelle grows into an extraordinary young woman. Unbeknownst to even Jaenelle, she is slowly growing her own court even though she is so set against becoming a queen. What makes Jaenelle also very special and different is that as her human followers grow she also has the undying support of the Kindred. The Kindred are the animals of the blood such as the unicorns, dragons, wolves and other creatures that will protect Jaenelle from all harm. That harm comes in the form of the skanky evil wench queen Dorothea, and her counterpart, the former wife of Saeten and, “I hope she rots in sewage” Hekatah. They have an idea of what Jaenelle can accomplish and need to stop her and control her. If only they truly knew what Jaenelle is capable of. No one knows, not even Saeten, and as Jaenelle continues to embrace Witch, she could become very unstable. Looks are very deceiving when it comes to Jaenelle and when she is backed into a corner or manipulated; she lashes out in a way that could destroy all three realms.<br /><br />Jaenelle is still a kind and gentle soul who longs to be a Healer. The one she saves most is Lucivar. Lucivar is able to escape the salt mines he was placed in as punishment. Lucivar was going to commit suicide and enter into Hell as a demon-dead, but Jaenelle saves him and from that he is free. He no longer has the ring of obedience and he can serve Witch as he has always longed for. Whereas Daemon wants to be Witch’s lover, Lucivar wants to be Witch’s brother and servant in everything else. The relationship Anne writes between Lucivar and Jaenelle is just as wonderful as Saeten and Jaenelle’s father and daughter relationship. We have two of these relationships that almost complete the triangle that Daemon’s biological mother, Tersa, first mentions in Queen of Darkness. The only one still unresolved and incomplete is the one of the two lovers of Daemon and Jaenelle/Witch. That is the main question that arises in Heir to the Shadows. Will Daemon and Jaenelle be reunited?<br /><br />Heir to the Shadows was much more comfortable to read than Daughter of the Blood. There are some scenes of torture, but it happens to the ones who have caused the most pain against Jaenelle and her family. Also, Anne gives us a taste of what is to come in Queen of Darkness, and what Jaenelle will be forced to do to save the world and bring peace across the land.<br /><br />Daughter of the Blood had me by the throat and wouldn’t let go. Heir to the Shadows allowed me breathe a bit, as if this was the calm before the storm that will be Queen of the Darkness. With that in mind, I have still embraced this world of the blood and the jewels and that of Jaenelle, Daemon, Lucivar and Saeten and their unknown paths that will be concluded in Queen of the Darkness.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18367620797633809101" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ShOHrWbY58oEH8M/Ud7RtdT1m/Q6yimOcvpyYMUh81HuccEXvKn/Xum9UhyD3gTAZ59GfmheGHTCEgGJBeCCsw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4LgjkOjPFGRa1rArhS0VFdhpOtK51pIMvbPrOnsl7P1E2mUqMr4M8Ld0IQhXLcBgawPnWOtCo/YNW5jTu+SdHw==')})
  }
//]]>
